Astral was supposed to face Escorpion Negro in a mask, but the comissions said no - Negro was Carlos Ibarro, who had lost his mask as Suriano (Carlos Ibarra) and wasn't allowed to put wager his mask again. He did appear to unmask for the crowd. Oborman replaced, but Astral lost his mask. (Both people originally scheduled for this match was unmasked.)

## 33 minutes. Tinieblas weighed 107 kg, Canek weighed 110 kg. First fall to Tinieblas in 10 minutes, second fall to Canek in 11 minutes, Canek win the third in 12 minutes after Tinieblas got the visual win with th ereferee out.

MORA (SUN) 04/22/1979 Toreo de Cuatro Caminos, Naucalpan, Estado de México [http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=522203451160728&set=a.461505387230535.102143.454597374588003&type=1 DJ Spectro, KO 1382, http://wrestlingclassics.com/cgi-bin/.ubbcgi/ultimatebb.cgi?ubb=get_topic;f=10;t=004610 Matt Farmer, RB, http://superluchas.com/2015/04/22/en-un-dia-como-hoy-1979-antonio-inoki-vs-canek-en-el-toreo-dos-caras-destapa-a-astro-rey/ SuperLuchas]
1) Ray Mendoza, Villano I b Ham Lee, Kurisu
## Kurisu and Ham Lee didn't work together.
2) Dos Caras b Astro Rey [mask]
## Astro was unmasked as Leonel Alberto Hernandez Lopez, 28 years old. Dos Caras took 2/3.
3) Perro Aguayo Sr. b Gran Hamada [UWA JLH]
## Title change. Perro is the 3rd known champion. 19 minutes (10/3/6). Perro at 88 kg, Hamada at 89. Perro took 1/3.
4) Ring Fujinami DRAW El Solitario [WWWF JH]
## Fujinami took 1, Solitario 2, double pin in the third. Ring kept the title. Solitario 92, Fujinami 94.
5) Antonio Inoki b Canek [NWF HEAVY]
## Inoki used karate chops early, which the fans felt was unethical in a title match. Both ended outside, and Canek used a chair for the first fall DQ in 13 minutes. Canek landed two topes in the second fall, but Inoki got in his enziguri and pinned Canek for the straight falls win after a suplex (9 minutes.) Inoki weighed in at 107 kg, Canek at 110 kg. Masami Soronaka was referee.
&& show named Dual Meet Mexico vs Japon. Box Y Lucha 1382 says this was a sell outa and one of the best shows of the year.

UNL (SUN) 07/15/1979 Arena Coliseo [Box Y Lucha 1394, http://wrestlingclassics.com/.ubb/ultimatebb.php?ubb=get_topic;f=10;t=004609 Matt Farmer]Attendance: 6000

3) Águila India, Gran Cochisse b Bruno Victoria, Manuel Robles [hair]
4) El Santo, Satoru Sayama DQ Adorable Rubi, Divino Roy
## straight falls
5) Américo Rocca  (c) DCOR Kung Fu [NWA WELTER]
## 26:15. Benito seconded Rocca (77 kg), Sayama seconded Kung Fu (76.2 kg) Fall 1 for Kung Fu (11:19), Fall 2 Rocca (3:37), third went to a DCOR when neither could make it back in after a Kung Fu plancha off the post (11:19). Kung Fu, who has a history of injuries, suffered a leg one in this match (so he hurt himself on a benefit show.) This match was later awarded match of the year (from Arena Coliseo) in Box Y Lucha.
&& Billed as show of the year, put on by the union. New gate record of 270,000.00. Scalping of the tickets was huge for this card. Tickets that were selling for $30.00 were being sold by scalpers for $150.00.
